NOMAD MTP004 Full Observation Plan

nomad_mtp004_merged.txt - Table data in text format

Occultation Start Time = UTC time at 0 or 250km tangent altitude - 30s

Occultation End Time = UTC time at 0 or 250km tangent altitude + 30s

Dayside Nadir Start Time = UTC terminator crossing time - 120s

Dayside Nadir End Time = UTC terminator crossing time + 120s

TC start times include 10s initialisation time

Occultation observation timings include SO reference periods but not initialisation period

Dayside Nadir times includes extra time before and after terminator crossing

UVIS only orbits are not yet split into 3 parts

Durations are in seconds, all other timings in UTC

LTP file used for this analysis: LEVF_M004_SOC_PLANNING.EVF

Occultation timings may vary from SOC by up to 2 seconds, due to rounding errors

Dayside Nadir timings may vary from SOC by up to 20 seconds, due to rounding errors

Colour code: Green = observation assigned to NOMAD in LTP, timings unchanged; Light Green = UVIS Split Dayside Nadir (Timings TBD); Orange = End time modified due to clash with occultation precooling; Cyan = Start time modified due to clash with previous occultation; Pink = Start and end times both modified
